  /** Converts a <button> to look like an <a> tag. */
  .linkify {
    display: inline;
    padding: 0;
    margin: 0;
    border: 0;
    background: 0;
    cursor: pointer;
  }
  h1, h2, h3, h4 {

    color: var(--chops-link-color);
    text-decoration: none;

    font-family: var(--chops-font-family);
  }
  a:hover, .linkify:hover {
    text-decoration: underline;
  }
  a.button, .button {
    /* Links that look like buttons. */
    display: inline-flex;
    align-items: center;
    justify-content: center;
    text-decoration: none;
    transition: filter 0.3s ease-in-out, box-shadow 0.3s ease-in-out;
  }
  a.button:hover, .button:hover {

  }

  }

  }
  textarea, select, input {
    box-sizing: border-box;
    font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
  }
  /* Note: decoupling heading levels from styles is useful for
  * accessibility because styles will not always line up with semantically
  * appropriate heading levels.

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

The following revision refers to this bug:



<span class="line"><!---->The following revision refers to this bug:<!----></span>



<br>





  



<span class="line"><!---->  <!----></span>





https://chromium.googlesource.com/angle/angle/+/b574643ef28c92fcea5122dd7a72acb42a514eed



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium.googlesource.com/angle/angle/+/b574643ef28c92fcea5122dd7a72acb42a514eed"><!---->https://chromium.googlesource.com/angle/angle/+/b574643ef28c92fcea5122dd7a72acb42a514eed<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





commit 



<span class="line"><!---->commit <!----></span>





b574643ef28c92fcea5122dd7a72acb42a514eed



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/b574643ef28c92fcea5122dd7a72acb42a514eed"><!---->b574643ef28c92fcea5122dd7a72acb42a514eed<!----></a>



<br>





Author: Geoff Lang <



<span class="line"><!---->Author: Geoff Lang &lt;<!----></span>





geofflang@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/geofflang@chromium.org"><!---->geofflang@chromium.org<!----></a>





>



<span class="line"><!---->&gt;<!----></span>



<br>





Date: Mon Apr 19 16:47:05 2021



<span class="line"><!---->Date: Mon Apr 19 16:47:05 2021<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





D3D11: Skip blits if there is no intersection of dest areas



<span class="line"><!---->D3D11: Skip blits if there is no intersection of dest areas<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Blit11 would clip the destination rectangle with the destination size



<span class="line"><!---->Blit11 would clip the destination rectangle with the destination size<!----></span>



<br>





but ignore the result. gl::ClipRectangle returns false when the



<span class="line"><!---->but ignore the result. gl::ClipRectangle returns false when the<!----></span>



<br>





rectangles do not intersect at all, indicating the blit can be skipped.



<span class="line"><!---->rectangles do not intersect at all, indicating the blit can be skipped.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This could lead to an out-of-bounds write to the GPU memory for the



<span class="line"><!---->This could lead to an out-of-bounds write to the GPU memory for the<!----></span>



<br>





destination texture.

Before a merge request will be considered, the following information is required to be added to this bug:



<span class="line"><!---->Before a merge request will be considered, the following information is required to be added to this bug:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





1. Does your merge fit within the Merge Decision Guidelines?



<span class="line"><!---->1. Does your merge fit within the Merge Decision Guidelines?<!----></span>



<br>





- Chrome: 



<span class="line"><!---->- Chrome: <!----></span>





https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromium/src.git/+/master/docs/process/merge_request.md#when-to-request-a-merge

<br>





2. Links to the CLs you are requesting to merge.



<span class="line"><!---->2. Links to the CLs you are requesting to merge.<!----></span>



<br>





3. Has the change landed and been verified on ToT?



<span class="line"><!---->3. Has the change landed and been verified on ToT?<!----></span>



<br>





4. Does this change need to be merged into other active release branches (M-1, M+1)?



<span class="line"><!---->4. Does this change need to be merged into other active release branches (M-1, M+1)?<!----></span>



<br>





5. Why are these changes required in this milestone after branch?



<span class="line"><!---->5. Why are these changes required in this milestone after branch?<!----></span>



<br>





6. Is this a new feature?



<span class="line"><!---->6. Is this a new feature?<!----></span>



<br>





7. If it is a new feature, is it behind a flag using finch?



<span class="line"><!---->7. If it is a new feature, is it behind a flag using finch?<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Chrome OS Only:



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome OS Only:<!----></span>

hello, kirtiar@ - we greatly appreciate your reports as well as your enthusiasm and desire to receive updates on and information about your reported issues. Please understand that those responding to your bugs reports are working on fixes for numerous (both internally discovered and externally reported) bugs in parallel as well as other Chrome development work. While the Chrome security team strives and does often achieve responding to inquires and comments in a super timely manner, it may not always be to your desired timeline. 



<span class="line"><!---->hello, kirtiar@ - we greatly appreciate your reports as well as your enthusiasm and desire to receive updates on and information about your reported issues. Please understand that those responding to your bugs reports are working on fixes for numerous (both internally discovered and externally reported) bugs in parallel as well as other Chrome development work. While the Chrome security team strives and does often achieve responding to inquires and comments in a super timely manner, it may not always be to your desired timeline. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Please allow me to address a few things here: the bug was filed on 15 April, so even if the fix was landed the same day, the bug would not be marked as allpublic by 15 May- as bugs aren't publicly disclosed in full until 14 weeks following when the fix was landed, as per VRP policies (



<span class="line"><!---->Please allow me to address a few things here: the bug was filed on 15 April, so even if the fix was landed the same day, the bug would not be marked as allpublic by 15 May- as bugs aren't publicly disclosed in full until 14 weeks following when the fix was landed, as per VRP policies (<!----></span>





https://www.google.com/about/appsecurity/chrome-rewards/index.html#rewards



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://www.google.com/about/appsecurity/chrome-rewards/index.html#rewards"><!---->https://www.google.com/about/appsecurity/chrome-rewards/index.html#rewards<!----></a>





).



<span class="line"><!---->).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Also, please understand that the 14-week disclosure policy is not just a policy for VRP rules sake, but it exists for user safety. This allows adequate and sufficient time  for stable channel release with the fix to be accessible and in place for all different user populations before we publicly disclose the details about the bug and how it can be exploited. This is for keeping users as safe as possible while trying to patch all the bugs as quickly as possible.  



<span class="line"><!---->Also, please understand that the 14-week disclosure policy is not just a policy for VRP rules sake, but it exists for user safety. This allows adequate and sufficient time  for stable channel release with the fix to be accessible and in place for all different user populations before we publicly disclose the details about the bug and how it can be exploited. This is for keeping users as safe as possible while trying to patch all the bugs as quickly as possible.  <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





As Ade mentioned above, you're obviously on the right path and also similar to many of our researchers in that you've had a string of rejected reports prior. This is quite common and you can check this out by reviewing all the public past reports. 



<span class="line"><!---->As Ade mentioned above, you're obviously on the right path and also similar to many of our researchers in that you've had a string of rejected reports prior. This is quite common and you can check this out by reviewing all the public past reports. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





I would also like to encourage you to re-review the Chrome VRP rules linked above and understand these are the conditions for participating in the Chrome VRP and are upheld for each and every researcher who submits bug reports. We want this process to be as mutually beneficial as possible (we reward your research and credit you for your findings, we benefit by having you report bugs to us which allows us to fix them and protect users before they can be disclosed and exploited) and would hate for your to keep committing if you feel there is an inequity here. 



<span class="line"><!---->I would also like to encourage you to re-review the Chrome VRP rules linked above and understand these are the conditions for participating in the Chrome VRP and are upheld for each and every researcher who submits bug reports. We want this process to be as mutually beneficial as possible (we reward your research and credit you for your findings, we benefit by having you report bugs to us which allows us to fix them and protect users before they can be disclosed and exploited) and would hate for your to keep committing if you feel there is an inequity here. <!----></span>



<br>





Again, we appreciate your submissions, but also have to uphold rules and conditions to be do our due diligence to try and protect the millions of people who use Chrome every day. 



<span class="line"><!---->Again, we appreciate your submissions, but also have to uphold rules and conditions to be do our due diligence to try and protect the millions of people who use Chrome every day. <!----></span>



<br>





Thank you and we do hope we can look forward to more reports from you in the future.



<span class="line"><!---->Thank you and we do hope we can look forward to more reports from you in the future.<!----></span>

          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }

          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;

          overflow: auto;

          position: relative;
        }

          z-index: 999;

          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;

          cursor: pointer;

        }
